final abstract class Mapping()
   public static const
      LOWER_DOMAIN, LOWER_RANGE,
      UPPER_DOMAIN, UPPER_RANGE,
      TITLE_DOMAIN, TITLE_RANGE
   private static const
      LOWER, UPPER, TITLE, FOLD

   private static load(d, r)
      local t, e
      t := table()
      e := create string(!r)
      every insert(t, ord(d), @e)
      return t
   end

   private static init()

   private static lookup(t, i)
      return \t[i] | Text.utf8_seq(i)
   end

   private static convert_with(s, t)
      local x
      s := need_ucs(s)
      x := String{ lookup(t, ord(s)) }
      return ucs(x)
   end

   private static char_seq(s, t)
      s := need_ucs(s)
      suspend !lookup(t, ord(s))
   end

   #
   # See `fold_chars`; this is the equivalent for the upper case
   # mapping.
   #
   public static upper_chars(s)
      return create char_seq(s, UPPER)
   end

   #
   # See `fold_chars`; this is the equivalent for the lower case
   # mapping.
   #
   public static lower_chars(s)
      return create char_seq(s, LOWER)
   end

   #
   # See `fold_chars`; this is the equivalent for the title case
   # mapping.
   #
   public static title_chars(s)
      return create char_seq(s, TITLE)
   end

   #
   # Return a co-expression, the results of which are the individual
   # characters that would comprise `string(fold(s))`.  For example,
   # ~
   #     fold_chars(u"Spa")
   # ~
   # generates 5 characters, namely "s", "p", "a", "s", "s".
   #
   # This function is useful for doing comparisons.  For example, the
   # `ipl.sort.convert_cmp` and `ipl.sort.coex_cmp` procedures can be
   # used to create a comparator function as follows :-
   # ~
   #     import ipl.sort
   #     ...
   #     f := convert_cmp(Mapping.fold_chars, coex_cmp())
   # ~
   # 
   # This comparator could then be used to compare strings directly
   # or perhaps with a `SortTable` :-
   # ~
   #     import datastruct
   #     ...
   #     f(u"Spa", u"SPASS")   # Gives 0 (ie, equal).
   #     ...
   #     t := SortTable(, f)
   #     t.insert(u"Gef", 99)
   #     t.member(u"GEFSS")    # 99
   #     t.member(u"GEF")     # also 99
   #     t.select(1)            # u"Gef"
   # ~
   #
   public static fold_chars(s)
      return create char_seq(s, FOLD)
   end

   #
   # Convert a ucs string using the upper case mapping.  Note that
   # this gives the same result as `Text.upper()`.
   #
   public static upper(s)
      return convert_with(s, UPPER)
   end

   #
   # Convert a ucs string using the lower case mapping.  Note that
   # this gives the same result as `Text.lower()`.
   #
   public static lower(s)
      return convert_with(s, LOWER)
   end

   #
   # Convert a ucs string using the title case mapping.
   #
   public static title(s)
      return convert_with(s, TITLE)
   end

   #
   # Convert a ucs string using the case folding mapping.
   #
   public static fold(s)
      return convert_with(s, FOLD)
   end
end
